 manmohan sih ne kaha, "maine khud teen betiyon kaa pita hone ke naate is ghatana ko shiddat se mahasoos kiya he, jaisaa ki aap main se prayek vyakti ne mahasoos kiya he
 My wife, my family and i are all involved in the concern being made for the brutal crime victim

 ICCR ne kaha he ki aane vaale varshon main bhi aise aayojanon ke aayojakon ke prastaav par bharat ke hai kamishan kii sifarish or pradhanmantri, videsh mantri or anya sambandhit mantralayon kii anushansa milegi to uskaa paalan kiya jayega
 Significantly, there has been a controversy over ICCR sponsoring air tickets of 4 Indian authors to participate in the Karachi Literature Festival
 yah festival 10 se 12 farvari tak chalaa
 According to ICCR Director General Amarendra Khatua, last Thursday, four well-known artists of the country, Mamang Dei, Urvashi Butalia, Saif Mehmood and Preeti Shenoy, were given an air ticket by the ICCR to Karachi for the festival
 kul kharch 1 lakh 60 hazaar rupee aayaa tha or rahane-khaane kaa intazaam aayojakon ne kiya tha
 In 2016, the government made a policy to send Indian artists to such festivals abroad

 gauratlab he ki ICCR dwaara ne karachi litarechar festival main hissaa lene ke liye 4 bhartiya lekhakon ke air tikat ko sponcer karne par vivaad khadaa ho gaya

 Standard SMS Charges Applicable The incidence of mob lynching is increasing continuously in the country
 rajasthan sarkaar ab is par kanoon banane kii taiyaari main he
 In this regard, the government has also introduced the bill in the Rajasthan Legislative Assembly
 is bill ke mutabik mob linching kii ghatnaon ko anjaam dene ke baad 7 saal se lekar aajeevan karawas or 25 hajaar rupee se lekar paanch lakh rupee tak ke jurmaane kaa bhi praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 According to the bill, to prevent lynching, a nodal officer will be brought in the state, which will be of the level of Inspector General of Police
 isse pehle rajya ke siem ashok gahalot ne bajet bhaashan ke dauraan ghoshnaa kar di thi ki balaatkaar, mob linching or honor kiling jaise maamalon par kathor kanoon banaaya jayega
 Information about this law will also be given in school syllabus
 ashok gahalot ne kaha ki 15-20 log ikattha ho jate hai or phir ek shaks ko buree tarah maarthe hai
 Increasing crime in the society has to be stopped
 gahalot ne vipaksh ke sadasyon se poocha ki kya aap logon ko mob linching kii ghatana se dukh nahin hota
 Opposition members also agreed to this
 iske baad ashok gahalot ne kaha, isi tarah honor kiling main bhi ladke-ladakiyon ko maar diya jaataa he
 For this he referred to an incident in Sirohi, in which a boy and a girl were burnt alive
 is ghatana ke bare main media ko bhi pataa nahin chal paaya
 In the Bihar elections, which have become a question of prestige, the BJP wants to try every recipe, which is also benefiting a little
 jaateey sameekaran kii ore bad chuke is chunaav se kaaryakartaaon main utsaah kii kami party alaakaman ko dikhne lagi he
 Therefore, the party has planned to send about two and three thousand workers to Bihar on 'pilgrimage'
 swatantraaa diwas samaaroh ke fouran baad is yojana par amal shuru ho jayega, jisaki mukammal taiyaari ho chuki he
 The BJP has prepared this plan with the aim of bringing this election back to the development agenda
 jisamen bijepi shasit chaar rajyon- gujarat, maharashtra, madhya pradesh or chhattisgarh kaa chayan kiya he
 Workers of Bihar BJP in groups of 600-700 in these states will be sent to these states in turn
 yah daura kareeb teen se chaar din kaa ek rajya main hoga
 In this, the BJP will show the picture of the development of its state to its own workers
 bihar bijepi ke in kaaryakartaaon ko mumbai main siddhivinayak to ujjain main mahakaal or gujarat main somnath aadi mandiron ke bhi darshan karaae jaaenge
 But their focus is to show the development happening in these states
 apane hi kaaryakartaaon ko vikaas dikhaane kii jaruratkyon?sawaal uthta he ki achaanak bihar chunaav se thik pehle bijepi ko apane hi kaaryakartaaon ko yah samajhane kii jarurat kyon aan padi he ki bijepi shasit rajyon main behtareen vikaas ho rahaa he or yahi model bihar main bhi apanaaya ja saktaa he
 Workers will be told and shown about 24-hour electricity in Maharashtra, the best roads in Madhya Pradesh, Gujarat etc
 iskaa makasad yah he ki bijepi ke kaaryakarta bihar lautakar bijepi shasit rajyon ke vikaas ke bare main janata ko bataaen

 aise main vikaas kaa agenda peeche chhot rahaa he, lekin tirthaton ke formule se kaaryakartaaon kaa manobal bhi badhaayaa jayega or vikaas kii tasviir dikhaakar unhen janata ko yah batalaane ke liye prerit kiya jayega
